    /*Scroll to top when arrow up clicked BEGIN*/
    $(window).scroll(function () {
        var height = $(window).scrollTop();
        if (height > 130) {
            $('#back2Top').fadeIn();
        } else {
            $('#back2Top').fadeOut();
